GT Equivalence Verification (MatSci20)

GT: c0*epsilon**c1 + c2*(T - c3)*sin(epsilon)
Candidates evaluated: 59
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the ground truth:

**GT: 5.889184448896621·ε³ + 2.8821771197066277·(T - 279.6235977851866)·sin(ε)**

This simplifies to: `c0·ε³ + c2·T·sin(ε) - c2·c3·sin(ε)`

The key basis functions are: **ε³**, **T·sin(ε)**, and **sin(ε)**.

Let me analyze each candidate:

### Candidate 1:
All terms have denominator (c1 + epsilon). Factor it out:
`[T·c0·ε + T·c2 + T·c3·sin(c4·ε+c5) + T·c6·ε·sin(c4·ε+c5) + c7 + c8·ε + c9·ε] / (c1 + ε)`

This is a rational function in ε. GT has ε³ which is polynomial - this can't produce ε³ as a standalone term. Setting c1=0 gives division by ε, which changes the structure. No way to get ε³ + T·sin(ε).
**Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 2:
Has terms like T·ε·(c1+ε)²/(c2+ε). Expanding: T·ε·(c1²+2c1ε+ε²)/(c2+ε). If c2=0, this becomes T·(c1²+2c1ε+ε²) = T·c1² + 2Tc1ε + Tε². This gives T·ε² but GT needs ε³ (no T). Also has sin terms divided by (c2+ε). Can't match.
**Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 3:
Terms: c0·ε/(c1+ε), c2·sin(...)/(c1+ε), c5·ε·sin(...)/(c1+ε), c7·ε·exp(T·c8)/(c1+ε), c9·ε²·exp(T·c8)/(c1+ε)

Has exp(T·c8) dependence on T, not linear T. Can't match T·sin(ε).
**Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 4:
`c0·sin(c1ε+c2) + c3·exp(Tc4)·exp(c5ε) + c6 + c7·exp(Tc4) + c8·exp(Tc4)`

Has exp(T·c4) - exponential in T, not linear. Can't produce T·sin(ε) or ε³.
**Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 5:
Has exp and log(T·c6+1) terms, |ε|. No ε³ or T·sin(ε) basis functions.
**Candidate 5 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 6:
`c0·ε + c1 + c2·log(c3ε+1) + c4·exp(c5·sin(c6ε + c7·log(Tc8+1) + c9))`

The exp(sin(...)) is highly nonlinear. Can't produce ε³ or T·sin(ε).
**Candidate 6 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 7:
`c0·ε^c1 + c2 + c3·ε + c4·log(c5·exp(Tc6 + c7ε) + 1)`

c0·ε^c1 with c1=3 gives ε³. The log term: log(c5·exp(Tc6+c7ε)+1). For large arguments, this ≈ Tc6+c7ε+ln(c5), but this is an approximation, not exact. We need T·sin(ε), which this can never produce.
**Candidate 7 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 8:
`c0·ε² + c1·exp(Tc2) + c3 + c4·exp(Tc5)·sin(c6ε+c7)`

Has ε² (not ε³) and exp(T·c) (not linear T). Can't match.
**Candidate 8 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 9:
`c0·sin(c1ε+c2) + c3·ε + c4·ε^c5·log(Tc6+1)·cos(c7ε+c8)`

Need ε³ and T·sin(ε). The term c4·ε^c5·log(Tc6+1)·cos(c7ε+c8): log(Tc6+1) ≠ T (not linear in T). Missing ε³.
**Candidate 9 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 10:
`c0·sin(c1ε+c2) + c3·ε + c4·ε·log(Tc5+1)·cos(c6ε+c7)`

log(T·c5+1) is not linear in T. Can't produce T·sin(ε). Missing ε³.
